                                      2 * THIS PROGRAM GIVES AN EXAMPLE OF USAGE OF THE DIRECT ACCESS
                                      3 * METHOD.  IT BUILDS A DAM FILE FROM A SEQUENTIAL FILE.
                                      4 * IT ALSO SHOWS AN EXAMPLE OF A SELF-RELOCATING PROGRAM USING
                                      5 * REGISTER NOTATION IN THE MACROS. IT ALSO USES CHANNEL 12

000000                                2 DAMEXT   CSECT
                                      3          ENTRY BEGTRK,NUMTRKS,XTNTINFO,TRKSCYL
000000                                4 R0       EQU   0
000001                                5 R1       EQU   1
000002                                6 R2       EQU   2
000003                                7 R3       EQU   3
000004                                8 R4       EQU   4
000005                                9 R5       EQU   5
000006                               10 R6       EQU   6

000008                               12 R8       EQU   8
000009                               13 R9       EQU   9
00000A                               14 R10      EQU   10
00000B                               15 R11      EQU   11
00000C                               16 R12      EQU   12
00000D                               17 R13      EQU   13
00000E                               18 R14      EQU   14
00000F                               19 R15      EQU   15
                                     20 *
                                     21 * EXIT CALLED BY $$B TRANSIENTS AS EXTENT(S) BEING PROCESSED.
                                     22 *
                                     23 * ENTRY IS VIA SVC 8 FROM THE TRANSIENT, AND EXIT RECEIVES CONTROL
                                     24 * WITH REGISTERS AND CONTEXT OF THE PROGRAM THAT ISSUED THE OPEN MACRO
                                     25 * THAT RESULTED IN THE EXTENT EXIT BEING CALLED.
                                     26 *
                                     27 * THIS MEANS WE HAVE NO ADDRESSABILITY, AND A VERY LIMITED SET OF
                                     28 * AVAILABLE REGISTERS WITH WHICH TO ESTABLISH * ADDRESSABILITY AND
                                     29 * SAVE THE OTHER REGISTERS.  NOR DO WE HAVE DOS RPG DOCUMENTATION
                                     30 * THAT WOULD LET US UNDERSTAND THE RPG PROGRAM CONTEXT WELL ENOUGH
                                     31 * TO KNOW WHICH REGISTERS COULD BE USED.
                                     32 *
                                     33 * NB--R13 DOES NOT POINT TO A SAVEAREA.
                                     34 *
                                     35 * SO WE'LL USE REGISTERS CLAIMED BY OPEN (R0&R1) AND HOPE FOR THE
                                     36 * BEST.  THIS APPROACH SHOULD WORK FOR OTHER LANGUAGES.
                                     37 *
000000 1801                          38          LR    R0,R1               SAVE POINTER TO EXTENT DESCRIPTOR
000002 0510                          39          BALR  R1,0                CREATE A BASE REGISTER
000004                               40          USING DAMEXTAD,R1         ESTABLISH TEMPORARY ADDRESSABILITY
000004 900F 10AC            000B0    41 DAMEXTAD STM   R0,R15,SAVERPGX     SAVE RPG REGISTERS
000008 18C1                          42          LR    R12,R1              TRANSFER ADDRESSING
                                     43          DROP  R1
000004                               44          USING DAMEXTAD,R12        MAKE PROGRAM ADDRESSABLE
00000A 1810                          45          LR    R1,R0               MAKE EXTENT INFO ADDRESSABLE
00000C D20D C0F8 1000 000FC 00000    46          MVC   XTNTINFO,0(R1)      GET 14-BYTE EXTENT INFO TABLE
                                     47 *
                                     48 *  DETERMINE EXECUTION PARTITION, FIND THE LUB FOR SYS004, THEN
                                     49 *  FIND THE PUB SO WE CAN DETERMINE THE DEVICE TYPE.
                                     50 *
000012 5810 0014            00014    51          L     R1,X'14'             GET ADDR OF THIS PART'N COMRG
000016 4820 102E            0002E    52          LH    R2,X'2E'(,R1)        GET PIK/PID OF THIS PARTITION

00027                  05  CD-DEPT         PIC 99.
00028                  05  FILLER          PIC X.
00029              02  FILLER              PIC X(77).
00030          FD  DAFILE
00031              LABEL RECORDS ARE STANDARD
00032              RECORDING MODE IS F
00033              BLOCK CONTAINS 300 CHARACTERS
00034              DATA RECORD IS DA-BLK.
00035          01  DA-BLK.
00036              02  REC OCCURS 4 TIMES.
00037                  05  FILLER          PIC XX.
00038                  05  REC-EMPNO       PIC XXX.
00039                  05  FILLER          PIC X(70).
00040          FD  PRINT-FILE
00041              LABEL RECORDS ARE OMITTED
00042              RECORDING MODE IS F
00043              RECORD CONTAINS 133 CHARACTERS
00044              DATA RECORD IS PRINTOUT.
00045          01  PRINTOUT.
00046              02  ASA                 PIC X.
00047              02  FILLER              PIC X(132).
00048          01  HEADING1.
00049              02  FILLER              PIC X.
00050              02  H1-TODAY            PIC X(8).
00051              02  FILLER              PIC X(25).
00052              02  H1-TITLE            PIC X(13).
     2


00053              02  FILLER              PIC X(66).
00054              02  H1-PAGE             PIC X(4).
00055              02  FILLER              PIC X.
00056              02  H1-PAGENUM          PIC ZZ9.
00057              02  FILLER              PIC X(12).
00058          01  DETAIL-LINE-LISTING.
00059              02  FILLER              PIC X.
00060              02  FILLER              PIC X(5).
00061              02  DL-EMPNO            PIC X(3).
00062              02  FILLER              PIC X(2).
00063              02  DL-REC              PIC X(75).
00064              02  FILLER              PIC X(47).
00065          WORKING-STORAGE SECTION.
00066          01  ACT-KEY.
00067              02  ACT-KEY-TRK    COMP PIC S9(8) SYNC.
00068              02  ACT-KEY-DEPT        PIC XX.
00069          01  FILLER.
00070              02  NUMTRKS        COMP PIC S9(8) SYNC.
00071              02  QUOTIENT       COMP PIC S9(8) SYNC.
00072              02  WS-TODAY            PIC X(8).
00073              02  WS-PAGENUM   COMP-3 PIC S999 VALUE ZERO.
00074              02  WS-EOF              PIC X VALUE 'N'.
00075              02  WS-EOP              PIC X.
00076              02  WS-NRF              PIC X.
00077          PROCEDURE DIVISION.
00078              OPEN INPUT READER
00079                   INPUT DAFILE
00080         *         I-O   DAFILE
00081                   OUTPUT PRINT-FILE.
00082              MOVE SPACES TO PRINTOUT.
00083              CALL 'DAMEXT' USING DAFILE, NUMTRKS.
00084              MOVE CURRENT-DATE TO WS-TODAY
00085              PERFORM HEADING-ROUTINE THRU HEADING-ROUTINE-EXIT.
00086              READ READER AT END MOVE 'Y' TO WS-EOF.
00087              PERFORM DETAIL-ROUTINE THRU DETAIL-ROUTINE-EXIT
00088                  UNTIL WS-EOF = 'Y'
00089              CLOSE READER, DAFILE, PRINT-FILE
00090              STOP RUN.
00091
00092          DETAIL-ROUTINE.
00093              IF WS-EOP = 'Y'
00094                  PERFORM HEADING-ROUTINE THRU HEADING-ROUTINE-EXIT.
00095              DIVIDE NUMTRKS INTO CD-DEPT GIVING QUOTIENT
00096                  REMAINDER ACT-KEY-TRK.
00097              MOVE CD-DEPT TO ACT-KEY-DEPT
00098              MOVE 'N' TO WS-NRF
00099              READ DAFILE
00100                 INVALID KEY MOVE 'Y' TO WS-NRF.
00101              IF WS-NRF = 'N'
00102         *    UPDATE THE BLOCK AT THIS POINT
00103         *    REWRITE DA-BLK
00104                  IF      CD-EMPNO = REC-EMPNO (1)
00105                      MOVE REC-EMPNO (1) TO DL-EMPNO
     3


00106                      MOVE REC (1)       TO DL-REC
00107                  ELSE IF CD-EMPNO = REC-EMPNO (2)
00108                      MOVE REC-EMPNO (2) TO DL-EMPNO
00109                      MOVE REC (2)       TO DL-REC
00110                  ELSE IF CD-EMPNO = REC-EMPNO (3)
00111                      MOVE REC-EMPNO (3) TO DL-EMPNO
00112                      MOVE REC (3)       TO DL-REC
00113                  ELSE IF CD-EMPNO = REC-EMPNO (4)
00114                      MOVE REC-EMPNO (4) TO DL-EMPNO
00115                      MOVE REC (4)       TO DL-REC
00116                  ELSE
00117                      MOVE CD-EMPNO                TO DL-EMPNO
00118                      MOVE '     RECORD NOT FOUND' TO DL-REC
00119              ELSE
00120                  MOVE CD-EMPNO                TO DL-EMPNO
00121                  MOVE '     RECORD NOT FOUND' TO DL-REC.
00122              PERFORM PRINT-LINE THRU PRINT-LINE-EXIT.
00123              READ READER AT END MOVE 'Y' TO WS-EOF.
00124          DETAIL-ROUTINE-EXIT.
00125              EXIT.
00126
00127          HEADING-ROUTINE.
00128              MOVE WS-TODAY        TO H1-TODAY
00129              MOVE 'DAM-RETRIEVAL' TO H1-TITLE
00130              MOVE 'PAGE'          TO H1-PAGE
00131              ADD 1 TO WS-PAGENUM
00132              MOVE WS-PAGENUM      TO H1-PAGENUM
00133              MOVE '1' TO ASA
00134              PERFORM PRINT-LINE THRU PRINT-LINE-EXIT
00135              MOVE '0' TO ASA
00136              MOVE 'N' TO WS-EOP.
00137          HEADING-ROUTINE-EXIT.
00138              EXIT.
00139
00140          PRINT-LINE.
00141              WRITE PRINTOUT AFTER POSITIONING ASA
00142                  EOP MOVE 'Y' TO WS-EOP.
00143              MOVE SPACES TO PRINTOUT.
00144          PRINT-LINE-EXIT.
00145              EXIT.
     4
